The header file src/spawn_sync.h (lines 134-236) defines the SyncProcessRunner interface. Additionally, src/permission/child_process_permission.cc implements permission checks that must be passed before child processes can be spawned. The null-byte validation mechanism is the primary defense against command injection attacks, as it prevents attackers from using null bytes to terminate environment variable assignments or command arguments early, which could allow arbitrary command execution or environment variable injection.
